class="col-sm-12"> <h2><a name="', '">Quadriceps</a></strong> (compound movements only) and <strong><a href="HipsWt#Gluteus">Gluteus Maximus</a></strong> for <strong>basic exercises</strong> for Adductor Magnus, Posterior Fibers. Compound Quadriceps exercises can be performed with a wide stance to exercise the Adductors of the Femur.</p><p>Range of motion is greater for the ischial fibers of Adductor Magnus when performing single leg presses with resting leg positioned down or lunges or single leg split squats with resting leg positioned back. This staggard leg position inhibits the hip from turning posteriorly so its involvement is emphasized. </p>\n</div><div class="col-sm-6">\n<ul> <li>Stretch <ul> <li><a href="../../Stretches/HipAdductors/BentoverAdductorMagnus">Bent-over</a> </li><li><a href="../../Stretches/HipAdductors/KneelingAdductorMagnus">Kneeling</a> </li><li><a href="../../Stretches/HipAdductors/LyingAdductorMagnus">Lying</a> </li><li><a href="../../Stretches/HipAdductors/SeatedSingleLegAdductorMagnus">Seated Single Leg</a> </li><li><a href="../../Stretches/HipAdductors/SeatedAdductorMagnusFloor">Seated</a> <ul> <li><a href="../../Stretches/HipAdductors/SeatedAdductorMagnus">Chair or Bench</a> </li></ul> </li></ul> </li></ul>\n</div></div>\n</div></div></div>\n<div class="container"><div class="row"><div class="col-sm-12"> <p>See <a href="HipsWt">Hips</a> for <a href="HipsWt#Abductors">Hip Abductors </a> (outer hip) and <a href="HipsWt#Hip">Hip Flexors</a>. </p><p>For <a href="../../Muscles/Popliteus">Popliteus</a>, see <a href="#']]

href="../../Muscles/Adductors">Adductor Magnus</a> (ischial fibers)</h2>\n</div></div></div>\n<div class="container"><div class="row"><div class="col-sm-12"> <div class="row"><div class="col-sm-6">\n<p>See <strong><a href="#Quadriceps">Quadriceps</a></strong> (compound movements only) and <strong><a href="HipsWt#Gluteus">Gluteus Maximus</a></strong> for <strong>basic exercises</strong> for Adductor Magnus, Posterior Fibers. Compound Quadriceps exercises can be performed with a wide stance to exercise the Adductors of the Femur.</p><p>Range of motion is greater for the ischial fibers of Adductor Magnus when performing single leg presses with resting leg positioned down or lunges or single leg split squats with resting leg positioned back. This staggard leg position inhibits the hip from turning posteriorly so its involvement is emphasized. </p>\n</div><div class="col-sm-6">\n<ul> <li>Stretch <ul> <li><a href="../../Stretches/HipAdductors/BentoverAdductorMagnus">Bent-over</a> </li><li><a href="../../Stretches/HipAdductors/KneelingAdductorMagnus">Kneeling</a> </li><li><a href="../../Stretches/HipAdductors/LyingAdductorMagnus">Lying</a> </li><li><a href="../../Stretches/HipAdductors/SeatedSingleLegAdductorMagnus">Seated Single Leg</a> </li><li><a href="../../Stretches/HipAdductors/SeatedAdductorMagnusFloor">Seated</a> <ul> <li><a href="../../Stretches/HipAdductors/SeatedAdductorMagnus">Chair or Bench</a> </li></ul> </li></ul> </li></ul>\n</div></div>\n</div></div></div>\n<div class="container"><div class="row"><div class="col-sm-12"> <p>See <a href="HipsWt">Hips</a> for <a href="HipsWt#Abductors">Hip Abductors </a> (outer hip) and <a href="HipsWt#Hip">Hip Flexors</a>. </p><p>For <a href="../../Muscles/Popliteus">Popliteus</a>, see <a href="#Hamstrings">Hamstrings exercises</a> (above).</p>\n</div></div></div>\n']]
